the complete call chain for how Firefox initiates a TLS connection from the networking layer (Necko) through to the cryptographic layer (NSS/Network Security Services).\\n\\n## Hop 1: HTTP Protocol Layer\\n\\n**File:** `netwerk/protocol/http/nsHttpConnection.cpp`\\n**Class:** `nsHttpConnection`\\n**Key Function:** `EnsureSSLSetupComplete()`\\n\\nThe HTTP connection object manages the lifecycle of an HTTP connection. When handling HTTPS requests, it creates a `TlsHandshaker` instance that orchestrates SSL setup. The handshaker is stored as `RefPtr<TlsHandshaker> mTlsHandshaker` and receives calls to `SetupSSL()` to configure TLS parameters before initiating the connection.\\n\\n**File:** `netwerk/protocol/http/TlsHandshaker.cpp`\\n**Class:** `TlsHandshaker`\\n**Key Functions:** \\n- `SetupSSL()` (line 72) - Initiates SSL configuration\\n- `InitSSLParams()` - Configures SSL parameters and versions\\n- `SetupNPNList()` - Builds ALPN/NPN protocol negotiation list\\n- `EnsureNPNComplete()` - Drives handshake forward asynchronously\\n\\nThe `TlsHandshaker` class is responsible for all TLS-specific configuration before the handshake begins. It determines which TLS versions to support, which cipher suites are available, and which application-level protocols (ALPN) to advertise.\\n\\n## Hop 2: Socket Provider Registration\\n\\n**File:** `netwerk/socket/nsSocketProviderService.cpp`\\n**Location:** Socket provider factory in `netwerk/socket/`\\n\\nThe socket provider service acts as a factory/registry that maps socket type strings (\\\"ssl\\\", \\\"starttls\\\", etc.) to their concrete implementations. For SSL connections, it provides the `nsSSLSocketProvider` implementation.\\n\\n## Hop 3: NSS I/O Layer Bridge\\n\\n**File:** `security/manager/ssl/nsSSLSocketProvider.cpp`\\n**Class:** `nsSSLSocketProvider`\\n**Key Function:** `NewSocket()` (line 28)\\n\\nThe SSL socket provider implements the `nsISocketProvider` interface. When `NewSocket()` is called, it delegates to the NSS I/O layer functions:\\n\\n**File:** `security/manager/ssl/nsNSSIOLayer.cpp`\\n**Class/Functions:**\\n- `nsSSLIOLayerHelpers` class (defines platform-specific SSL method tables)\\n- `nsSSLIOLayerHelpers::Init()` - Initializes the custom I/O layer methods\\n- `nsSSLIOLayerNewSocket()` (line 1247) - Creates a new NSPR PRFileDesc with custom I/O handlers\\n- `nsSSLIOLayerAddToSocket()` (line 1790) - Wraps an existing socket with SSL I/O methods\\n- `nsSSLIOLayerConnect()` (line 163) - Connection handler registered in I/O method table\\n\\nThese functions create NSPR (Netscape Portable Runtime) file descriptors with custom I/O layer methods that intercept all socket operations (read, write, connect, close, etc.) to perform SSL/TLS operations. A `NSSSocketControl` instance is created to manage TLS-specific state.\\n\\n**File:** `security/manager/ssl/NSSSocketControl.cpp`\\n**Class:** `NSSSocketControl`\\n**Key Functions:**\\n- `StartTLS()` - Initiates TLS on an existing connection\\n- `DriveHandshake()` (line 242) - Drives the NSS handshake state machine forward\\n- `SetHandshakeCallbackListener()` - Registers callbacks for handshake progress\\n\\n## Hop 4: NSS Cryptographic Core\\n\\n**File:** `security/nss/lib/ssl/sslsecur.c`\\n**Key Functions:**\\n- `SSL_ForceHandshake()` (line 383) - The main entry point that drives the TLS handshake\\n- `ssl_SecureConnect()` (line 692) - Establishes secure connection\\n- `SSL_ResetHandshake()` (line 176) - Resets handshake state\\n\\nWhen `SSL_ForceHandshake()` is called on a PRFileDesc, it executes NSS's internal TLS handshake state machine, repeatedly processing records and advancing through handshake states until the handshake completes or fails.\\n\\n**File:** `security/nss/lib/ssl/ssl3con.c`\\n**Key Functions:**\\n- `ssl_BeginClientHandshake()` (line 113) - Initializes client-side handshake\\n- `ssl3_HandleClientHello()` (line 9254) - Server-side ClientHello message handling\\n- `ssl3_HandleClientHelloPart2()` (line 9646) - Continuation of ClientHello processing\\n\\nThese functions implement the actual TLS protocol state machine, handling ClientHello/ServerHello messages, key exchange, certificate verification, and record protection setup.\\n\\n**File:** `security/nss/lib/ssl/tls13con.c`\\n**Purpose:** TLS 1.3-specific protocol implementation when negotiated\\n\\n## Complete Call Chain\\n\\n```\\nnsHttpConnection::EnsureSSLSetupComplete()\\n  ↓\\nTlsHandshaker::SetupSSL()\\n  ├─ TlsHandshaker::InitSSLParams()\\n  └─ TlsHandshaker::SetupNPNList()\\n      ↓\\nnsSSLSocketProvider::NewSocket()\\n  ↓\\nnsSSLIOLayerNewSocket()\\n  ↓\\nnsSSLIOLayerAddToSocket()\\n  ├─ Create NSSSocketControl\\n  └─ Register I/O layer methods\\n      ↓\\nnsSSLIOLayerConnect() [via custom I/O layer]\\n  ↓\\nNSSSocketControl::DriveHandshake()\\n  ↓\\nSSL_ForceHandshake(PRFileDesc*)\\n  ├─ ssl_BeginClientHandshake() [client-side]\\n  └─ ssl3_HandleClientHello() [server-side]\\n      ↓\\nTLS Record Processing & Encryption\\n  (ssl3con.c / tls13con.c handle record layer)\\n```\\n\\n## Key Integration Points\\n\\n1. **NSPR File Descriptor Wrapping:** Firefox wraps TCP sockets with custom NSPR I/O methods, creating a layered file descriptor stack where each layer intercepts operations.\\n\\n2. **Asynchronous Handshake:** The `TlsHandshaker` and `NSSSocketControl` classes work together to drive the handshake asynchronously using callbacks, allowing Firefox to remain responsive.\\n\\n3. **Platform Abstraction:** `nsSSLIOLayerHelpers` provides platform-specific implementations of socket operations, abstractions for getting/setting socket options, and platform-dependent TLS features.\\n\\n4. **Certificate Validation:** Before the handshake completes, `NSSSocketControl` coordinates with `SSLServerCertVerification` to validate the server's certificate chain.\\n\\n5. **ALPN/NPN Negotiation:** progress\\n\\n## Hop 4: NSS Cryptographic Core\\n\\n**File:** `security/nss/lib/ssl/sslsecur.c`\\n**Key Functions:**\\n- `SSL_ForceHandshake()` (line 383) - The main entry point that drives the TLS PRFileDesc, it executes NSS's internal TLS handshake state machine, repeatedly processing records and advancing through handshake states until the handshake completes or fails.\\n\\n**File:** └─ ssl3_HandleClientHello() [server-side]\\n      ↓\\nTLS Record Processing & Encryption\\n  (ssl3con.c / tls13con.c handle record layer)\\n```\\n\\n## Key Integration Points\\n\\n1. **NSPR File Descriptor Wrapping:** Firefox wraps TCP sockets with custom NSPR I/O methods, creating a layered file descriptor stack where each layer intercepts operations.\\n\\n2. **Asynchronous Handshake:** The `TlsHandshaker` and `NSSSocketControl` classes work together to drive the handshake asynchronously using callbacks, allowing Firefox to remain responsive.\\n\\n3. **Platform Abstraction:** `nsSSLIOLayerHelpers` provides platform-specific implementations of socket operations, abstractions for getting/setting socket options, and platform-dependent TLS features.\\n\\n4. **Certificate Validation:** Before the handshake completes, `NSSSocketControl` coordinates with `SSLServerCertVerification` to validate the server's certificate chain.\\n\\n5. **ALPN/NPN Negotiation:** `TlsHandshaker::SetupNPNList()` configures which HTTP versions (h2 for HTTP/2, h2c, http/1.1) to negotiate, which NSS transmits during the ClientHello extension.\\n\\n## Repository\\n\\nAll files are NSS as a submodule at `security/nss/`, but the modern Firefox build system may link against a system NSS or bundled version.
